	 <!-- Wrapping the Recaptcha create method in a javascript function -->
<script type="text/javascript">
		var widgetCaptcha;
		function showRecaptcha(element, selectByThisClass) {
			$("#submit-captcha").removeClass('submit-captcha-login').removeClass('submit-contacto-listado');
			dataLayer.push ({ 
				'event': 'trackEvent',
				'eventCategory': 'CAPTCHA', 
				'eventAction': 'Impresion', 
				'eventLabel': $('body').attr('id') || $('.contenedor-listado').attr('id') || ''
			});
			if (typeof widgetCaptcha == "undefined"){
			    widgetCaptcha =	grecaptcha.render(element, {
					'sitekey' : '6LdPAy0UAAAAAI-7KxrDvxJjwQMIMYT3mI4oUmXZ',
					'theme' : 'white',
					'callback' : function(response){
						reCaptchaResponse = response;
						verifyCallback();
					}
				});
			}else{
				grecaptcha.reset(widgetCaptcha);
			}
			if (selectByThisClass){
				$("#submit-captcha").addClass(selectByThisClass);
			}
		}
		function verifyCallback(){
			$("#submit-captcha").submit();
		}
		function submitCaptchaCallback(){
			dataLayer.push ({ 
				'event': 'trackEvent',
				'eventCategory': 'CAPTCHA', 
				'eventAction': 'Validacion', 
				'eventLabel': $('body').attr('id') || $('.contenedor-listado').attr('id') || ''
			});
		};
		function recaptchaUrlParameter(){
			return "g-recaptcha-response=" + grecaptcha.getResponse();
			
		}
		$(function(){
			$('#id-div-captcha .mfp-close, #id-div-captcha .mfp-bg').on('click', function () {
				realestate().ui.popup.close();
			});
		});
</script>
